# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
+ UpdateBuffer(String) in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
d1 $== d2 && bool_eq(s1, s2) in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
b1 $== b2 && List.equal(Todo.eq, ts1, ts2) in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

# Add a todo item #
let add: Model -> [Todo] =

type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
+ UpdateBuffer(String) in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =

type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
+ UpdateBuffer(String) in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
d1 $== d2 && bool_eq(s1, s2) in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
b1 $== b2 && List.equal(Todo.eq, ts1, ts2) in

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
+ UpdateBuffer(String) in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
d1 $== d2 && bool_eq(s1, s2) in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
b1 $== b2 && List.equal(Todo.eq, ts1, ts2) in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

# Add a todo item #
let add: Model -> [Todo] =
  fun model ->
    case model

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
+ UpdateBuffer(String) in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
d1 $== d2 && bool_eq(s1, s2) in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
b1 $== b2 && List.equal(Todo.eq, ts1, ts2) in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

# Add a todo item #
let add: Model -> [Todo] =
  fun model ->
    case model
    | (buffer, todos

  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
+ UpdateBuffer(String) in

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
+ UpdateBuffer(String) in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
d1 $== d2 && bool_eq(s1, s2) in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
b1 $== b2 && List.equal(Todo.eq, ts1, ts2) in

let add: Model -> [Todo] =
  fun model ->
    case model
    | (buffer, todos) =>
        if

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
+ UpdateBuffer(String) in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
d1 $== d2 && bool_eq(s1, s2) in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
b1 $== b2 && List.equal(Todo.eq, ts1, ts2) in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

let add: Model -> [Todo] =
  fun model ->

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
+ UpdateBuffer(String) in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
d1 $== d2 && bool_eq(s1, s2) in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
b1 $== b2 && List.equal(Todo.eq, ts1, ts2) in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

let add: Model -> [Todo] =
  fun model ->
    case model
    | (buffer, todos) =>
        if buffer $== ""

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
+ UpdateBuffer(String) in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
d1 $== d2 && bool_eq(s1, s2) in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
b1 $== b2 && List.equal(Todo.eq, ts1, ts2) in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

  fun model ->
    case model
    | (buffer, todos) =>
        if buffer $== ""
        let new

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
+ UpdateBuffer(String) in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
d1 $== d2 && bool_eq(s1, s2) in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
b1 $== b2 && List.equal(Todo.eq, ts1, ts2) in

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
+ UpdateBuffer(String) in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
d1 $== d2 && bool_eq(s1, s2) in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
b1 $== b2 && List.equal(Todo.eq, ts1, ts2) in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

let add: Model -> [Todo] =
  fun model ->
    case model
    | (buffer, todos) =>
        if buffer $== ""
        let new_todo = (buffer, false

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
+ UpdateBuffer(String) in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
d1 $== d2 && bool_eq(s1, s2) in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
b1 $== b2 && List.equal(Todo.eq, ts1, ts2) in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

# Add a todo item #
let add: Model -> [Todo] =
  fun model ->
    case model
    | (buffer, todos) =>
        if buffer $== ""
        let new_todo = (buffer, false) in

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
+ UpdateBuffer(String) in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
d1 $== d2 && bool_eq(s1, s2) in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
b1 $== b2 && List.equal(Todo.eq, ts1, ts2) in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

# Add a todo item #
let add: Model -> [Todo] =
  fun model ->
    case model
    | (buffer, todos) =>
        if buffer $== ""
        let new_todo = (buffer, false) in
        todos @

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
+ UpdateBuffer(String) in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
d1 $== d2 && bool_eq(s1, s2) in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
b1 $== b2 && List.equal(Todo.eq, ts1, ts2) in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

# Add a todo item #
let add: Model -> [Todo] =
  fun model ->
    case model
    | (buffer, todos) =>
        if buffer $== ""
        let new_todo = (buffer, false) in
        todos @ [new

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
+ UpdateBuffer(String) in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
d1 $== d2 && bool_eq(s1, s2) in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
b1 $== b2 && List.equal(Todo.eq, ts1, ts2) in

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
+ UpdateBuffer(String) in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
d1 $== d2 && bool_eq(s1, s2) in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
b1 $== b2 && List.equal(Todo.eq, ts1, ts2) in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

# Add a todo item #
let add: Model -> [Todo] =
  fun model ->
    case model
    | (buffer, todos) =>
        if buffer $== ""
        let new_todo = (buffer, false) in
        todos @ [new_todo]

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
+ UpdateBuffer(String) in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
d1 $== d2 && bool_eq(s1, s2) in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
b1 $== b2 && List.equal(Todo.eq, ts1, ts2) in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

# Add a todo item #
let add: Model -> [Todo] =
  fun model ->
    case model
    | (buffer, todos) =>
        if buffer $== ""
        let new_todo = (buffer, false) in
        todos @ [new_todo]
        ![]

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
+ UpdateBuffer(String) in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
d1 $== d2 && bool_eq(s1, s2) in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
b1 $== b2 && List.equal(Todo.eq, ts1, ts2) in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

# Add a todo item #
let add: Model -> [Todo] =
  fun model ->
    case model
    | (buffer, todos) =>
        if buffer $== ""
        let new_todo = (buffer, false) in
        todos @ [new_todo]
        ![]

# A todo has a description and a status #
type Todo = (String, Bool) in

# A description input buffer and a todo list #
type Model = (String, [Todo]) in

type Action =
  + AddTodo
  + RemoveTodo(Int)
  + ToggleTodo(Int)
+ UpdateBuffer(String) in

let Todo.eq: (Todo, Todo) -> Bool =
  fun (d1, s1), (d2, s2) ->
d1 $== d2 && bool_eq(s1, s2) in

let Model.eq: (Model, Model) -> Bool =
  fun (b1, ts1), (b2, ts2) ->
b1 $== b2 && List.equal(Todo.eq, ts1, ts2) in

let Model.init: Model = ("", []) in

# Add a todo item #
let add: Model -> [Todo] =
  fun model ->
    case model
    | (buffer, todos) =>
        if buffer $== ""
        let new_todo = (buffer, false) in
        todos @ [new_todo]
        ![]
    ![]
